<P class="p600 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(n)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">the renewal of the registration pursuant to Article 50d and the date from which that renewal takes effect;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p582 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(o)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">the determination of the expiry of the registration pursuant to Article 50d(8);</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(p)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft99">a declaration of surrender by the holder pursuant to Article 51(1);</SPAN></P>
<P class="p710 ft57"><SPAN class="ft65">(q)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft137">the date of submission and the particulars of an application for a declaration of invalidity under Article 52, of a counterclaim for a declaration of invalidity pursuant to Article 84(5) or of an appeal brought pursuant to Article 55;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p711 ft57"><SPAN class="ft65">(r)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft138">the date and particulars of the final decision on the application for a declaration of invalidity pursuant to Article 53, of the final decision on a counterclaim for a declaration of invalidity pursuant to Article 86(3), of the final decision on an appeal pursuant to Article 55, or of any other termination of proceedings pursuant, to those Articles;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft56"><SPAN class="ft68">(s)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft94">the cancellation of the entry concerning the representative recorded pursuant to paragraph 2, point (e);</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">(t)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft139">the modification or cancellation from the Register of the items referred to in paragraph 3, points (l), (m) and (n).</SPAN></P>
<P class="p712 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">(u)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft140">the revocation of a decision or the cancellation of an entry in the Register pursuant to Article 66h, where the revocation concerns a decision or the cancellation concerns an entry which has been published.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p602 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The Executive Director may determine that items other than those referred to in paragraphs 2 and 3 are to be entered in the Register.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p677 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The Register may be maintained in electronic form. The Office shall collect, organise, make public and store the items referred to in paragraphs 1, 2 and 3, including any personal data, for the purposes laid down in paragraph 8. The Office shall keep the Register easily accessible for public inspection.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The holder of a registered EU design shall be notified of any change in the Register.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p679 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">7.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The Office shall, where access to the Register is not restricted pursuant to Article 74(5), provide, by electronic means, certified or uncertified extracts from the Register upon request.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p678 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">8.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The processing of the data concerning the entries set out in paragraphs 2 and 3, including any personal data, shall take place for the purposes of:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p713 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">administering the applications, registrations, or both, as described in this Regulation and any acts adopted pursuant to it;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p714 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">maintaining a public Register for inspection by, and the information of, public authorities and economic operators, in order to enable them to exercise the rights conferred on them by this Regulation and be informed about the existence of prior rights belonging to third parties;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p715 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">producing reports and statistics enabling the Office to optimise its operations and improve the functioning of the system for registration of EU designs.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p677 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">9.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">All the data, including personal data, concerning the entries set out in paragraphs 2 and 3 of this Article shall be considered to be of public interest and may be accessed by any third party except to the extent that Article 50(2) provides otherwise. The entries in the Register shall be kept for an indefinite period.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p323 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(89)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft94">the following articles are inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft56">‘Article 72a</P>
<P class="p557 ft62">Database</P>
<P class="p559 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">In addition to the obligation to keep a Register as set out in Article 72, the Office shall collect and store in an electronic database all the particulars provided by holders or any other party to the proceedings pursuant to this Regulation or acts adopted pursuant to it.</SPAN></P>

	<TD class="tr30 td111"><SPAN class="p263 ft63">ELI: <A href="http://data.europa.eu/eli/reg/2024/2822/oj">http://data.europa.eu/eli/reg/2024/2822/oj</A></SPAN> </TD>

<P class="p584 ft63"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The electronic database may include personal data, beyond those included in the Register pursuant to Article 72, to the extent that such data are required by this Regulation or by acts adopted pursuant to it. The collection, storage and processing of personal data shall serve the purposes of:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p716 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">administering the applications, registrations, or both, as described in this Regulation and in acts adopted pursuant to it;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p567 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft93">accessing the information necessary for conducting the relevant proceedings more easily and efficiently;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p585 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">communicating with the applicants and other parties to the proceedings; and</SPAN></P>
<P class="p575 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">producing reports and statistics enabling the Office to optimise its operations and improve the functioning of the system.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p629 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">The Executive Director shall determine the conditions of access to the database and the manner in which the contents, other than the personal data referred to in paragraph 2 of this Article but including the data listed in Article 72, may be made available.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p668 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">Access to the personal data referred to in paragraph 2 shall be restricted and such data shall not be made publicly available unless the party concerned has expressly consented.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p584 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">All data shall be kept indefinitely. However, the party concerned may request the removal of any personal data from the database after 18 months from the expiry of the registered EU design or the closure of the relevant inter partes procedure. The party concerned shall have the right to obtain the correction of inaccurate or erroneous data at any time.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p717 ft56">Article 72b</P>
<P class="p634 ft62">Online access to decisions</P>
<P class="p572 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The decisions of the Office regarding registered EU designs shall be made available online for the information and consultation of the general public. Any party to the proceedings that led to the adoption of the decision may request the removal of any personal data included in the decision.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p577 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The Office may provide online access to judgments of national and Union courts related to its tasks in order to raise public awareness of intellectual property matters and promote convergence of practices. The Office shall respect the conditions of the initial publication with regard to personal data.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p242 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(90)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">Article 73 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p571 ft56">‘Article 73</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Periodical publications</P>
<P class="p543 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The Office shall periodically publish:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p718 ft57"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft108">a European Union Designs Bulletin containing publications of entries made in the Register, as well as other particulars relating to registrations of EU designs the publication of which is required by this Regulation or by acts adopted pursuant to it;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p576 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft98">an Official Journal of the Office containing notices and information of a general character issued by the Executive Director, as well as any other information relevant to this Regulation or its implementation.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p543 ft56">The publications referred to in the first subparagraph, points (a) and (b), may be effected by electronic means.</P>
<P class="p668 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The European Union Designs Bulletin shall be published in a manner and at a frequency to be determined by the Executive Director.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p629 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">The Official Journal of the Office shall be published in the languages of the Office. However, the Executive Director may determine that certain items are to be published in the Official Journal of the Office in the official languages of the Union.’;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p601 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">paragraph 4 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p720 ft56">‘4. Where the files are inspected pursuant to paragraph 2 or 3, the following parts of the file shall be excluded from inspection:</P>
<P class="p721 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">documents relating to exclusion or objection pursuant to Article 169 of Regulation (EU) 2017/1001;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p722 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">draft decisions and opinions, and all other internal documents used for the preparation of decisions and opinions;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p723 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">parts of the file which the party concerned showed a special interest in keeping confidential before the request for inspection of the files was made, unless inspection of such part of the file is justified by overriding legitimate interests of the party seeking inspection.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p556 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the following paragraph is added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p724 ft63">‘5. Where the registration is subject to a deferment of publication pursuant to Article 50(1), access to the Register for persons other than the holder of the registered EU design shall be limited to the name of the holder, the name of any representative, the date of filing and registration, the file number of the application and the indication that publication is deferred. In such cases, the certified or uncertified extracts from the register shall contain only the name of the holder, the name of any representative, the date of filing and registration, the file number of the application and the indication that publication is deferred, except where the request for extracts has been made by the holder or by the holder’s representative.’;</P>
<P class="p334 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(93)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft94">the following articles are inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft56">‘Article 74a</P>
<P class="p557 ft62">Procedures for the inspection of files</P>
<P class="p669 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">Inspection of the files of registered EU designs requested pursuant to Article 74(3) shall be of the technical means of storage of the files. Such inspection shall take place online. The Executive Director shall determine the means of inspection.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p687 ft79">2. Where the request for inspection of the files relates to an application for a registered EU design or to a registered EU design which are subject to deferment of publication in accordance with Article 50 or which, being subject to such deferment, have been surrendered before or on the date of expiry of that period, the request shall contain evidence that:</P>
<P class="p537 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">the applicant for or holder of the EU design has consented to the inspection; or</SPAN></P>
<P class="p596 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the person requesting the inspection has established a legitimate interest in the inspection of the file.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p629 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">Upon request, inspection of the files shall be effected by means of electronic copies of file documents. The Office shall also, upon request, issue certified or uncertified copies of the application for a registered EU design by electronic means.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p571 ft56">Article 74b</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Communication of information contained in the files</P>
<P class="p587 ft63">Subject to the restrictions provided for in Article 74, the Office may, upon request, communicate information from any file of any procedure relating to an EU design application or to a registered EU design.</P>
<P class="p543 ft56">Article 74c</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Keeping of files</P>
<P class="p587 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The Office shall keep the files of any procedure relating to EU design applications and to registered EU designs. The Executive Director shall determine the form in which those files are to be kept.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p635 ft79"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft109">Where the files are kept in electronic format, the electronic files, or </SPAN><NOBR>back-up</NOBR> copies thereof, shall be kept indefinitely. The original documents filed by parties to the proceedings, and forming the basis of such electronic files, shall be disposed of after a period following their reception by the Office, which shall be determined by the Executive Director.</P>
<P class="p725 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">Where, and to the extent that, files or parts of the files are kept in any form other than electronically, documents or items of evidence constituting part of such files shall be kept for at least five years from the end of the year in which:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p571 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the application is rejected or withdrawn;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p585 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the registration of the EU design expires definitively;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p571 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the surrender of the registered EU design is entered in the Register pursuant to Article 51;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p585 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the registered EU design is definitively removed from the Register.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p242 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(94)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">Article 75 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p571 ft56">‘Article 75</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Administrative cooperation</P>
<P class="p572 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Unless otherwise provided for in this Regulation or in national law, the Office and the courts or authorities of the Member States shall upon request give assistance to each other by communicating information or opening files for inspection. Where the Office opens files to inspection by courts, public prosecutors’ offices or central industrial property offices, the inspection shall not be subject to the restrictions laid down in Article 74.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p585 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The Office shall not charge fees for the communication of information or the opening of files for inspection.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p242 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(95)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">the following article is inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p571 ft56">‘Article 75a</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Conferral of implementing powers regarding administrative cooperation</P>
<P class="p572 ft63">The Commission shall adopt implementing acts setting out the detailed arrangements for the exchange of information between the Office and the authorities of the Member States and for the opening of files for inspection as referred to in Article 75, taking into account the restrictions to which the inspection of files relating to EU design applications or registrations is subject, pursuant to Article 74, when they are opened to third parties. Those implementing acts shall be adopted in accordance with the examination procedure referred to in Article 109(2).’;</P>
<P class="p242 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(96)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">Article 76 is deleted;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p222 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(97)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft94">Article 77 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft56">‘Article 77</P>
<P class="p557 ft62">General principles of representation</P>
<P class="p596 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">Subject to paragraph 2, no person shall be compelled to be represented before the Office.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p562 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Without prejudice to paragraph 3, second subparagraph, of this Article, natural or legal persons having neither their domicile nor their principal place of business or a real and effective industrial or commercial establishment in the EEA shall be represented before the Office in accordance with Article 78(1) in all proceedings provided for by this Regulation, other than the filing of an application for a registered EU design.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p679 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Natural or legal persons having their domicile or principal place of business or a real and effective industrial or commercial establishment in the EEA may be represented before the Office by an employee.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p604 ft63">An employee of a legal person to which this paragraph applies may also represent other legal persons which have economic connections with the first legal person, even if those other legal persons have neither their domicile nor their principal place of business nor a real and effective industrial or commercial establishment within the EEA.</P>
<P class="p562 ft63">Employees who represent persons within the meaning of this paragraph shall, at the request of the Office or, where appropriate, of the party to the proceedings, provide the Office with a signed authorisation for insertion in the files.</P>
<P class="p602 ft56">4. Where there is more than one applicant or more than one third party acting in common, a common representative shall be appointed.’;</P>
<P class="p333 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(98)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft94">Article 78 is amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft56">(a) paragraphs 1 to 6 are replaced by the following:</P>
<P class="p726 ft56">‘1. Representation of natural or legal persons in proceedings before the Office under this Regulation may only be undertaken by any of the following:</P>
<P class="p727 ft57"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft108">a legal practitioner qualified in one of the States party to the EEA Agreement and having the place of business within the EEA, to the extent that the legal practitioner is entitled, within that State, to act as a representative in industrial property matters;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p638 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">professional representatives whose names appear on the list of professional representatives referred to in Article 120(1), point (b), of Regulation (EU) 2017/1001;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p728 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">professional representatives whose names appear on the special list of professional representatives for design matters referred to in paragraph 4.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p729 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The professional representatives referred to in paragraph 1, point (c), shall only be entitled to represent third persons in proceedings on design matters before the Office.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p730 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Representatives acting before the Office shall, at the request of the Office or, where appropriate, of the other party to the proceedings, provide the Office with a signed authorisation for insertion on the files.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p731 ft63"><SPAN class="ft63">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The Office shall establish and maintain a special list of professional representatives in design matters. Any natural person who fulfils all the following conditions may be entered on that list:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p732 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">being a national of one of the States party to the EEA Agreement;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p641 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">having the place of business or employment in the EEA;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p643 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">being entitled to represent natural or legal persons in design matters before the Benelux Office for Intellectual Property or before the central industrial property office of a State party to the EEA Agreement.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p733 ft63">Where the entitlement referred to in the first subparagraph, point (c), is not conditional upon the requirement of having special professional qualifications, a person applying to be entered on the list who acts in design matters before the Benelux Office for Intellectual Property or a central industrial property office shall have habitually so acted for at least five years.</P>

<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p12 ft2">Prop. 2024/25:108</P>
<P class="p140 ft2">Bilaga 1</P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t18">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr9 td151"><SPAN class="p13 ft56">OJ L, 18.11.2024</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr9 td152"><SPAN class="p13 ft59">EN</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr28 td153"><SPAN class="p13 ft75">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr28 td154"><SPAN class="p13 ft75">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p734 ft57">However, persons whose professional qualification to represent natural or legal persons in design matters before the Benelux Office for Intellectual Property or a central industrial property office is officially recognised in accordance with the regulations laid down by the State concerned shall not be required to have exercised the profession.</P>
<P class="p649 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft85">Entry on the list of professional representatives in design matters shall be effected upon request, accompanied by a certificate furnished by the Benelux Office for Intellectual Property or the central industrial property office of the Member State concerned, indicating that the conditions laid down in paragraph 4 are fulfilled. The entries in the list of professional representatives in design matters shall be published in the Official Journal of the Office.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p735 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The Executive Director may grant an exemption from any of the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p736 ft57"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft113">the requirement set out in paragraph 4, first subparagraph, point (a), in the case of highly qualified professionals, provided that the requirements set out in paragraph 4, first subparagraph, points (b) and (c), are fulfilled;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p737 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft96">the requirement set out in paragraph 4, second subparagraph, if the person applying to be entered on the list furnishes proof that he or she has acquired the required qualification in another way.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p571 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft93">paragraph 7 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p738 ft79">‘7. A person may be removed from the list of professional representatives in design matters at the request of that person or when that person is no longer in a capacity to act as a professional representative. The amendments of the list of professional representatives in design matters shall be published in the Official Journal of the Office.’;</P>
<P class="p594 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the following paragraph is added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p647 ft63">‘8. Representatives acting before the Office shall be entered in the database referred to in Article 72a and obtain an identification number. The Office may require the representative to prove the real and effective nature of their establishment or employment at any of the addresses identified. The Executive Director may determine the formal requirements for obtaining an identification number, in particular for associations of representatives, and for the entries of the representatives in the database.’;</P>
<P class="p246 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(99)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">the following article is inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p636 ft56">‘Article 78a</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Delegation of power regarding professional representation</P>
<P class="p668 ft56">The Commission is empowered to adopt delegated acts in accordance with Article 109a to supplement this Regulation by specifying:</P>
<P class="p655 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the conditions and the procedure for the appointment of a common representative as referred to in Article 77(4);</SPAN></P>
<P class="p739 ft57"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft141">the conditions under which employees referred to in Article 77(3) and professional representatives referred to in Article 78(1) shall file with the Office a signed authorisation in order to undertake representation, and the content of that authorisation;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p740 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the circumstances in which a person may be removed from the list of professional representatives in design matters referred to in Article 78(7).’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p361 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(100)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 79 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p636 ft56">‘Article 79</P>
<P class="p741 ft62">Application of Union rules on jurisdiction and the recognition and enforcement of judgments in civil and commercial matters</P>
<P class="p659 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Unless otherwise specified in this Regulation, the Union rules on jurisdiction and the recognition and enforcement of judgments in civil and commercial matters shall apply to proceedings relating to EU designs and applications for registered EU designs, as well as to proceedings relating to simultaneous and successive actions on the basis of EU designs and national designs.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p600 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">In the case of proceedings in respect of the actions and claims referred to in Article 81 of this Regulation:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p742 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">Articles 4 and 6, Article 7, points 1, 2, 3 and 5, and Article 35 of Regulation (EU) No 1215/2012 of the European Parliament and of the Council (*) shall not apply;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p715 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Articles 25 and 26 of Regulation (EU) No 1215/2012 shall apply subject to the limitations set out in Article 82(4) of this Regulation;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p743 ft57"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft113">the provisions of Chapter II of Regulation (EU) No 1215/2012 which are applicable to persons domiciled in a Member State shall apply also to persons who do not have a domicile in any Member State but have an establishment therein.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p555 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">References in this Regulation to Regulation (EU) No 1215/2012 shall include, where appropriate, the Agreement between the European Community and the Kingdom of Denmark on jurisdiction and the recognition and enforcement of judgments in civil and commercial matters done on 19 October 2005.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p583 ft57"><SPAN class="ft65">(*)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft97">Regulation (EU) No 1215/2012 of the European Parliament and of the Council of 12 December 2012 on jurisdiction and the recognition and enforcement of judgments in civil and commercial matters (OJ L 351, 20.12.2012, p. 1).’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p312 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(101)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">in Article 80, paragraph 5 is deleted;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p200 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(102)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 82 is amended as follows:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p554 ft56">(a) paragraph 1 is replaced by the following:</P>
<P class="p744 ft63">‘1. Subject to the provisions of this Regulation and to any provisions of Regulation (EU) No 1215/2012 applicable by virtue of Article 79 of this Regulation, proceedings in respect of the actions and claims referred to in Article 81 of this Regulation shall be brought in the courts of the Member State in which the defendant is domiciled or, if the defendant is not domiciled in any of the Member States, in any Member State in which the defendant has an establishment.’;</P>
<P class="p556 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft93">paragraph 4 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p745 ft56">‘4. By way of derogation from paragraphs 1, 2 and 3 of this Article:</P>
<P class="p746 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 25 of Regulation (EU) No 1215/2012 shall apply if the parties agree that a different EU design court is to have jurisdiction;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p722 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 26 of Regulation (EU) No 1215/2012 shall apply if the defendant enters an appearance before a different EU design court.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p366 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(103)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">in Article 84, the following paragraphs are added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p555 ft63">‘5. The EU design court with which a counterclaim for a declaration of invalidity of a registered EU design has been filed shall not proceed with the examination of the counterclaim, until either the interested party or the court has informed the Office of the date on which the counterclaim was filed. The Office shall record that information in the Register in accordance with Article 72(3), point (q). If an application for a declaration of invalidity of the registered EU design had been filed with the Office before the counterclaim was filed, the court shall be informed thereof by the Office and stay the proceedings in accordance with Article 91(1) until the decision on the application is final or the application is withdrawn.</P>
<P class="p627 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The EU design court hearing a counterclaim for a declaration of invalidity of a registered EU design may, on application by the right holder of the registered EU design and after hearing the other parties, stay the proceedings and request the defendant to submit an application for a declaration of invalidity to the Office within a time limit which the court shall determine. If the application is not made within the time limit, the proceedings shall continue and the counterclaim shall be deemed withdrawn. Article 91(3) shall apply.’;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p187 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(104)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 86 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p636 ft56">‘Article 86</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Judgments of invalidity</P>
<P class="p668 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">Where in proceedings before an EU design court, the EU design has been put in issue by way of a counterclaim for a declaration of invalidity:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p660 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">if any of the grounds mentioned in Article 25 are found to prejudice the maintenance of the EU design, the court shall declare the EU design invalid;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p747 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">if none of the grounds mentioned in Article 25 is found to prejudice the maintenance of the EU design, the court shall reject the counterclaim.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p673 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">An EU design court shall reject a counterclaim for a declaration of invalidity of a registered EU design if a decision taken by the Office relating to the same subject matter and cause of action and involving the same parties has already become final.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p630 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Where an EU design court has given a judgment which has become final on a counterclaim for a declaration of invalidity of a registered EU design, a copy of the judgment shall be sent to the Office without delay, either by the court or by any of the parties to the national proceedings. The Office or any other interested party may request information about such judgment. The Office shall enter the judgment in the Register in accordance with Article 72(3), point (r).’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p147 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(105)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">in Article 88, paragraph 2 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p609 ft56">‘2. On all design matters not covered by this Regulation, an EU design court shall apply the applicable national law.’;</P>
<P class="p187 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(106)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 89 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p636 ft56">‘Article 89</P>
<P class="p634 ft62">Sanctions in actions for infringement</P>
<P class="p577 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Where an EU design court finds that the defendant has infringed or threatened to infringe an EU design, it shall, unless there are special reasons for not doing so, issue an order prohibiting the defendant from proceeding with the acts which infringed or would infringe the EU design. It shall also take such measures in accordance with its national law as are aimed at ensuring that that prohibition is complied with.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p631 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The EU design court may also apply measures or orders available under the applicable law which it deems appropriate in the circumstances of the case.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p361 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(107)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">in Article 90, paragraph 3 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p630 ft63">‘3. An EU design court whose jurisdiction is based on Article 82(1), (2), (3) or (4) of this Regulation shall have jurisdiction to grant provisional measures, including protective measures, which, subject to any necessary procedure for recognition and enforcement pursuant to Chapter III of Regulation (EU) No 1215/2012, are applicable in the territory of any Member State. No other court shall have such jurisdiction.’;</P>
<P class="p350 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(108)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 93 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p636 ft56">‘Article 93</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Supplementary provisions on the jurisdiction of national courts other than EU design courts</P>
<P class="p569 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Within the Member State whose courts have jurisdiction under Article 79(1), the courts which would have jurisdiction ratione loci and ratione materiae in the case of actions relating to a national design right in that Member State shall have jurisdiction for actions relating to EU designs other than the actions referred to in Article 81.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p666 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">Actions relating to an EU design, other than the actions referred to in Article 81, for which no court has jurisdiction pursuant to Article 79(1) and paragraph 1 of this Article may be heard before the courts of the Member State in which the Office has its seat.’;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p556 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft91">the following paragraph is inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p749 ft56">‘4a. Without prejudice to paragraph 4:</P>
<P class="p750 ft57"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft108">any application or declaration relating to an application for a registered EU design may be filed in the language used for filing the application for a registered EU design or in the second language indicated by the applicant in that application;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p751 ft57"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft108">any application or declaration relating to an application for a registered EU design other than an application for a declaration of invalidity pursuant to Article 52 or a declaration of surrender pursuant to Article 51 may be filed in one of the languages of the Office.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p752 ft63">However, when any of the forms provided by the Office as referred to in Article 66d is used, such forms may be used in any of the official languages of the Union, provided that the form is completed in one of the languages of the Office, as far as textual elements are concerned.’;</P>
<P class="p554 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft93">the following paragraphs are added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p753 ft63">‘6. Without prejudice to paragraphs 3 and 5 and unless provided for otherwise, in written proceedings before the Office a party may use any language of the Office. If the language chosen is not the language of the proceedings, the party shall supply a translation into that language within one month of the date of the submission of the original document. Where the applicant for a registered EU design is the sole party to proceedings before the Office and the language used for the filing of the application for the registered EU design is not one of the languages of the Office, the translation may also be filed in the second language indicated by the applicant in the application.</P>
<P class="p754 ft56">7. The Executive Director shall determine the manner in which translations are to be certified.’;</P>

<P class="p554 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the requisite standards of translations to be filed with the Office.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p187 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(113)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 99 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p567 ft56">‘Article 99</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Publication and entries in the Register</P>
<P class="p620 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">All information the publication of which is prescribed by this Regulation or an act adopted pursuant to this Regulation shall be published in all the official languages of the Union.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p618 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">All entries in the Register shall be made in all the official languages of the Union.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p676 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">In cases of doubt, the text in the language of the Office in which the application for the registered EU design was filed shall be authentic. If the application was filed in an official language of the Union other than one of the languages of the Office, the text in the second language indicated by the applicant shall be authentic.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p246 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(114)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 100 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p655 ft56">‘Article 100</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Supplementary powers of the Executive Director</P>
<P class="p659 ft63">In addition to the powers conferred upon the Executive Director by Article 157(4), point (o), of Regulation (EU) 2017/1001, the Executive Director shall exercise the powers conferred under Article 36(5), Article 37(1), Article 41(5), Article 42(2), Article 62(2), Article 65(5), Articles 66, 66c and 66e, Article 72(4), Article 72a(3), Article 73, Article 74a(1), Articles 74c and 78, Article 98(7), Article <NOBR>-106aa,</NOBR> Article <NOBR>-106ab(1)</NOBR> and Articles <NOBR>-106ac</NOBR> and <NOBR>-106ad</NOBR> of this Regulation in accordance with the criteria set out in this Regulation and in the acts adopted pursuant to this Regulation.’;</P>
<P class="p351 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(115)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 101 is deleted;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p187 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(116)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Articles 102, 103 and 104 are replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p655 ft56">‘Article 102</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Competence</P>
<P class="p609 ft56">For taking decisions in connection with the procedures laid down in this Regulation, the following shall be competent:</P>
<P class="p618 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">examiners;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p567 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft93">the Department in charge of the Register;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p655 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Invalidity Divisions;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p567 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft93">Boards of Appeal.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p655 ft56">Article 103</P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Examiners</P>
<P class="p609 ft56">The examiners shall be responsible for taking decisions on behalf of the Office in relation to an application for a registered EU design.</P>
<P class="p618 ft56">Article 104</P>
<P class="p634 ft62">The Department in charge of the Register</P>
<P class="p673 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">In addition to the powers conferred upon it by Regulation (EU) 2017/1001, the Department in charge of the Register shall be responsible for taking decisions in respect of entries in the Register under this Regulation and other decisions required by this Regulation which do not fall within the competence of the examiners or an Invalidity Division.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p682 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The Department in charge of the Register shall also be responsible for maintaining the list of professional representatives in design matters.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p303 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(117)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">in Article 105, the following paragraph is added:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p567 ft56">‘3. Decisions relating to costs or to procedures shall be taken by a single member of the Invalidity Division.’;</P>

<P class="p222 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(118)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the following article is inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft56">‘Article 105a</P>
<P class="p557 ft62">Conferral of implementing powers regarding decisions taken by a single member</P>
<P class="p669 ft57">The Commission shall adopt implementing acts specifying the exact types of decisions that are to be taken by a single member as referred to in Article 105(3). Those implementing acts shall be adopted in accordance with the examination procedure referred to in Article 109(2).’;</P>
<P class="p334 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(119)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 106 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft56">‘Article 106</P>
<P class="p557 ft62">Boards of Appeal</P>
<P class="p604 ft63">In addition to the powers conferred upon it by Article 165 of Regulation (EU) 2017/1001, the Boards of Appeal shall be responsible for deciding on appeals against decisions of the instances of the Office referred to in Article 102, points (a), (b) and (c) of this Regulation, in connection with the procedures laid down in this Regulation.’;</P>
<P class="p366 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(120)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the following article is inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p601 ft56">‘Article <NOBR>-106a</NOBR></P>
<P class="p557 ft62">Delegation of power regarding the Boards of Appeal</P>
<P class="p604 ft63">The Commission is empowered to adopt delegated acts in accordance with Article 109a of this Regulation to supplement it by specifying the details concerning the organisation of the Boards of Appeal in proceedings relating to designs under this Regulation where such proceedings require the Boards of Appeal to be organised differently from what is laid down in the delegated acts adopted pursuant to Article 168 of Regulation (EU) 2017/1001.’;</P>
<P class="p756 ft104"><SPAN class="ft63">(121)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft144">the following Section is added in Title XI: ‘ S e c t i o n 3</SPAN></P>
<P class="p689 ft62">F e e s a n d t h e i r p a y m e n t</P>
<P class="p606 ft56">Article <NOBR>-106aa</NOBR></P>
<P class="p557 ft62">Fees and charges and due date</P>
<P class="p677 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The Executive Director shall lay down the amount to be charged for any services rendered by the Office other than those set out in the Annex, as well as the amount to be charged for publications issued by the Office. The amounts of charges shall be set in euro and shall be published in the Official Journal of the Office. The amount of each charge shall not exceed what is necessary to cover the costs of the specific service rendered by the Office.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p679 ft63"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Fees and charges in respect of which the due date is not specified in this Regulation shall be due on the date of receipt of the request for the service for which the fee or the charge is incurred.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p664 ft63">With the consent of the Budget Committee, the Executive Director may determine which of the services mentioned in the first subparagraph is not to be dependent upon the advance payment of the corresponding fees or charges.</P>
<P class="p556 ft56">Article <NOBR>-106ab</NOBR></P>
<P class="p665 ft62">Payment of fees and charges</P>
<P class="p599 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">Fees and charges due to the Office shall be paid by the methods of payment determined by the Executive Director with the consent of the Budget Committee.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p678 ft56">The methods of payment determined pursuant to the first subparagraph shall be published in the Official Journal of the Office. All payments shall be made in euro.</P>
<P class="p757 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">Payments through means of payment other than those referred to in paragraph 1 shall be considered not to have been made and the amount which has been paid shall be refunded.</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t17">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr30 td110"><SPAN class="p262 ft63">44/50</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr30 td111"><SPAN class="p263 ft63">ELI: <A href="http://data.europa.eu/eli/reg/2024/2822/oj">http://data.europa.eu/eli/reg/2024/2822/oj</A></SPAN> </TD>

<P class="p682 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">Payments shall contain the necessary information to enable the Office to establish immediately the purpose of the payment.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p633 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">If the purpose of the payment referred to in paragraph 2 cannot immediately be established, the Office shall require the person making the payment to notify it in writing of that purpose within a certain period. If the person does not comply with the request within that period, the payment shall be considered not to have been made and the amount which has been paid shall be refunded.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p655 ft56">Article <NOBR>-106ac</NOBR></P>
<P class="p544 ft62">Deemed date of payment</P>
<P class="p621 ft56">The Executive Director shall establish the date on which payments are to be considered to have been made.</P>
<P class="p567 ft56">Article <NOBR>-106ad</NOBR></P>
<P class="p634 ft62">Insufficient payments and refund of excess payments</P>
<P class="p758 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">A time limit for payment shall be considered to have been observed only if the full amount of the fee or charge has been paid in due time. If the fee or charge is not paid in full, the amount which has been paid shall be refunded after the period for payment has expired.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p692 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The Office shall, however, in so far as is possible within the time remaining before the end of the period for payment, give the person making the payment the opportunity to pay the amount lacking.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p620 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">With the consent of the Budget Committee, the Executive Director may waive action for the enforced recovery of any sum due where the sum to be recovered is minimal or where such recovery is too uncertain.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p574 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">Where an excessive sum is paid to cover a fee or a charge, the excess shall be refunded.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p187 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(122)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">in Article 106d, paragraph 3 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p673 ft57">‘3. The Office shall provide information on international registrations referred to in paragraph 2 in the form of an electronic link to the searchable database of international registrations of designs maintained by the International Bureau.’;</P>
<P class="p187 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(123)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 106e is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p567 ft56">‘Article 106e</P>
<P class="p634 ft62">Examination of grounds for refusal</P>
<P class="p659 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Where the Office finds, in the course of carrying out an examination of an international registration, that the design for which protection is sought does not correspond to the definition in Article 3, point (1), of this Regulation, that the design is contrary to public policy or to accepted principles of morality, or that the design constitutes an improper use of any of the items listed in Article 6ter of the Paris Convention, or of badges, emblems and escutcheons other than those covered by the said Article 6ter and which are of particular public interest in a Member State, it shall send to the International Bureau a notification of refusal not later than six months from the date of publication of the international registration, specifying the grounds for refusal pursuant to Article 12(2) of the Geneva Act.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p698 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Where the holder of the international registration is obliged to be represented before the Office pursuant to Article 77(2), the notification referred to in paragraph 1 of this Article shall contain a reference to the obligation of the holder to appoint a representative as referred to in Article 78(1).</SPAN></P>
<P class="p659 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The Office shall specify a time limit by which the holder of the international registration may renounce the international registration in respect of the Union, limit the international registration in respect of the Union to one or some of the industrial designs or submit observations, and, where appropriate, shall appoint a representative. The period shall start on the day on which the Office issues the notification of refusal.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p759 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">If the holder fails to appoint a representative within the period referred to in paragraph 3, the Office shall refuse the effects of the international registration.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p633 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Where the holder submits observations that satisfy the Office within the specified period, the Office shall withdraw the refusal and notify the International Bureau in accordance with Article 12(4) of the Geneva Act. Where, pursuant to Article 12(2) of the Geneva Act, the holder does not submit observations that satisfy the Office within the specified period, the Office shall confirm the decision refusing protection for the international registration. That decision shall be subject to appeal in accordance with Articles 66 to 72 of Regulation (EU) 2017/1001 in conjunction with Article 55(2) of this Regulation.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p369 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(124)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the following article is added in Title XIa:</SPAN></P>

<P class="p334 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(125)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Articles 107 and 108 are deleted;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p366 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(126)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 109 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p556 ft56">‘Article 109</P>
<P class="p665 ft62">Committee Procedure</P>
<P class="p748 ft63"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The Commission shall be assisted by the Committee on Implementation Rules established by Regulation (EU) 2017/1001. That committee shall be a committee within the meaning of Regulation (EU) No 182/2011.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p554 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">Where reference is made to this paragraph, Article 5 of Regulation (EU) No 182/2011 shall apply.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p191 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(127)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the following article is inserted:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p596 ft56">‘Article 109a</P>
<P class="p557 ft62">Exercise of the delegation</P>
<P class="p561 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">The power to adopt delegated acts is conferred on the Commission subject to the conditions laid down in this Article.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p760 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The power to adopt delegated acts referred to in Articles 47b, 53a, 55a, 64a, 65a, 66a, 66d, 66f, 66i, 67c, 78a and </SPAN><NOBR>-106a</NOBR> shall be conferred on the Commission for an indeterminate period of time from 8 December 2024.</P>
<P class="p627 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">The delegation of power referred to in Articles 47b, 53a, 55a, 64a, 65a, 66a, 66d, 66f, 66i, 67c, 78a and </SPAN><NOBR>-106a</NOBR> may be revoked at any time by the European Parliament or by the Council. A decision to revoke shall put an end to the delegation of the power specified in that decision. It shall take effect the day following the publication of the decision in the Official Journal of the European Union or at a later date specified therein. It shall not affect the validity of any delegated acts already in force.</P>
<P class="p562 ft63"><SPAN class="ft63">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">Before adopting a delegated act, the Commission shall carry out consultations with experts, including experts designated by each Member State in accordance with the principles laid down in the Interinstitutional Agreement of</SPAN></P>
<P class="p761 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">13</SPAN><SPAN class="ft93">April 2016 on Better </SPAN><NOBR>Law-Making.</NOBR></P>
<P class="p623 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">As soon as it adopts a delegated act, the Commission shall notify it simultaneously to the European Parliament and to the Council.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p579 ft63"><SPAN class="ft65">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft89">A delegated act adopted pursuant to Articles 47b, 53a, 55a, 64a, 65a, 66a, 66d, 66f, 66i, 67c, 78a or </SPAN><NOBR>-106a</NOBR> shall enter into force only if no objection has been expressed either by the European Parliament or by the Council within a period of two months of notification of that act to the European Parliament and the Council or if, before the expiry of that period, the European Parliament and the Council have both informed the Commission that they will not object. That period shall be extended by two months at the initiative of the European Parliament or of the Council.’;</P>
<P class="p490 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(128)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">Article 110 is deleted;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p191 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(129)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">in Article 110a, paragraph 5, the second sentence is deleted;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p762 ft129"><SPAN class="ft63">(130)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft128">the following article is inserted: ‘Article 110b</SPAN></P>
<P class="p763 ft62">Evaluation</P>
<P class="p610 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft88">By 1 January 2030, and every five years thereafter, the Commission shall evaluate the implementation of this Regulation.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p764 ft57"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft110">The Commission shall forward the evaluation report together with its conclusions drawn on the basis of that report to the European Parliament, the Council and the Management Board. The findings of the evaluation shall be made public.’;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p477 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(131)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">in Article 111, paragraph 2 is replaced by the following:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p544 ft56">‘2. Applications for registered EU designs may be filed at the Office from 1 April 2003.’;</P>
<P class="p479 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">(132)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">the Annex as set out in Annex I to this Regulation is added.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p765 ft56">Article 2</P>
<P class="p479 ft56">Regulation (EC) No 2246/2002 is repealed with effect from 1 May 2025.</P>
<P class="p766 ft63">References to the repealed Regulation shall be construed as references to Regulation (EC) No 6/2002 and shall be read in accordance with the correlation table set out in Annex II to this Regulation.</P>
<P class="p767 ft56">Article 3</P>
<P class="p480 ft56">This Regulation shall enter into force on the twentieth day following that of its publication in the Official Journal of the European Union.</P>
<P class="p477 ft56">It shall apply from 1 May 2025.</P>
<P class="p766 ft63">However, Article 1, points (21), (22), (24), (26), (27), (28), (29), (30), (32)(b), (34)(b), (37), (40), (42), (45), (46), (49), (52), (54), (56), (58), (61), (63), (65), (66), (70), (72), (74), (76), (78), (80)(b), (81), (85), (88) in so far as it relates to Article 72(3), points (a), (e), (f) and (m), (90), (98)(b), (111), (113) and (123) shall apply from 1 July 2026.</P>
<P class="p768 ft56">This Regulation shall be binding in its entirety and directly applicable in all Member States.</P>

<P class="p771 ft63">‘ANNEX</P>
<P class="p772 ft62">Amounts of fees as referred to in Article <NOBR>-106aa(1)</NOBR></P>
<P class="p490 ft56">The fees to be paid to the Office under this Regulation shall be as follows (in EUR):</P>
<P class="p773 ft104"><SPAN class="ft63">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft130">Application fee referred to in Article 36(4): EUR 350.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p774 ft104"><SPAN class="ft63">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft130">Individual designation fee for an international registration referred to in Article 106c: EUR 62 per design.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p775 ft104"><SPAN class="ft63">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft130">Fee for deferment of publication referred to in Article 36(4): EUR 40.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p776 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">Additional application fee in respect of each additional design included in a multiple application referred to in Article 37(2):</SPAN></P>
<P class="p493 ft56">EUR 125.</P>
<P class="p492 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">Additional fee for deferment of publication in respect of each additional design included in a multiple application that is subject to deferment of publication referred to in Article 37(2):</SPAN></P>
<P class="p493 ft56">EUR 20.</P>
<P class="p366 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">Renewal fee referred to in Article 50d(1), (3) and (9):</SPAN></P>
<P class="p494 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">for the first period of renewal: EUR 150 per design;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p491 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">for the second period of renewal: EUR 250 per design;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p494 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">for the third period of renewal: EUR 400 per design;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p494 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">for the fourth period of renewal: EUR 700 per design.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p366 ft56"><SPAN class="ft63">7.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft116">Individual renewal fee for an international registration referred to in Article 106c:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p494 ft56"><SPAN class="ft65">(a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft92">for the first period of renewal: EUR 62 per design;</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p787 ft4">Prop. 2024/25:108 Bilaga 2</P>
<P class="p788 ft2">118</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p789 ft37">Sammanfattning av promemorian Ändringar i EU:s formskyddsförordning</P>
<P class="p790 ft6">I promemorian föreslås ändringar i mönsterskyddslagen med anledning av revideringen av EU:s förordning om gemenskapsformgivning, som nu bland annat byter namn till förordningen om <NOBR>EU-formgivning.</NOBR></P>
<P class="p791 ft2">Det föreslås att bestämmelserna om straffansvar och förverkande av egendom i mönsterskyddslagen inte ska gälla vid intrång i en EU- formgivning om produkterna endast passerar genom EU utan att släppas ut på den inre marknaden. Vidare föreslås att regleringen om att Patent- och registreringsverket får ta ut en avgift för att vidarebefordra en ansökan om registrering av en formgivning på <NOBR>EU-nivå</NOBR> ska tas bort. De hänvisningar till gemenskapsformgivning som görs i lagen föreslås ändras till <NOBR>EU-formgivning.</NOBR></P>
<P class="p792 ft2">Lagändringarna föreslås träda i kraft den dag regeringen bestämmer.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_119">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p12 ft1">Lagförslagen i promemorian</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p12 ft4">Prop. 2024/25:108 Bilaga 3</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p793 ft15">Förslag till lag om ändring i mönsterskyddslagen (1970:485)</P>
<P class="p794 ft4">Härigenom föreskrivs att 1, 43, 50 och 51 §§ och rubriken närmast före 50 § mönsterskyddslagen (1970:485) ska ha följande lydelse.</P>

<P class="p802 ft2">43 §<SPAN class="ft17">2</SPAN></P>
<P class="p796 ft2">Patent- och marknadsdomstolen är rätt domstol i</P>
<P class="p62 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft33">mål och ärenden enligt denna lag om de inte ska handläggas enligt lagen (1974:371) om rättegången i arbetstvister, och</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t49">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td172"><SPAN class="p49 ft2">2. mål som avses i artikel 81 i</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td25"><SPAN class="p31 ft2">2. mål som avses i artikel 81 i</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td172"><SPAN class="p49 ft2">rådets förordning (EG) nr 6/2002</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td25"><SPAN class="p13 ft2">rådets förordning (EG) nr 6/2002</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td172"><SPAN class="p803 ft16"><SPAN class="ft19">om </SPAN>gemenskapsformgivning.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td25"><SPAN class="p13 ft3"><SPAN class="ft2">om </SPAN><NOBR>EU-formgivning.</NOBR></SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p61 ft6">Det som sägs i rättegångsbalken om inskränkning av en domstols behörighet i fråga om tvist som ska tas upp i annan ordning än inför domstol ska inte tillämpas i fråga om ett yrkande om informationsföreläggande eller intrångsundersökning.</P>

<P class="p793 ft15">Förslag till lag om ändring i mönsterskyddslagen (1970:485)</P>
<P class="p794 ft4">Härigenom föreskrivs att 1, 43, 50 och 51 §§ och rubriken närmast före 50 § mönsterskyddslagen (1970:485) ska ha följande lydelse.</P>

<P class="p796 ft2">I denna lag avses med</P>

<P class="p802 ft2">43 §<SPAN class="ft17">2</SPAN></P>
<P class="p796 ft2">Patent- och marknadsdomstolen är rätt domstol i</P>
<P class="p62 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft33">mål och ärenden enligt denna lag om de inte ska handläggas enligt lagen (1974:371) om rättegången i arbetstvister, och</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t49">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td172"><SPAN class="p49 ft2">2. mål som avses i artikel 81 i</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td25"><SPAN class="p31 ft2">2. mål som avses i artikel 81 i</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td172"><SPAN class="p49 ft2">rådets förordning (EG) nr 6/2002</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td25"><SPAN class="p13 ft2">rådets förordning (EG) nr 6/2002</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td172"><SPAN class="p803 ft16"><SPAN class="ft19">om </SPAN>gemenskapsformgivning.</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td25"><SPAN class="p13 ft3"><SPAN class="ft2">om </SPAN><NOBR>EU-formgivning.</NOBR></SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p61 ft6">Det som sägs i rättegångsbalken om inskränkning av en domstols behörighet i fråga om tvist som ska tas upp i annan ordning än inför domstol ska inte tillämpas i fråga om ett yrkande om informationsföreläggande eller intrångsundersökning.</P>

<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p12 ft4">Prop. 2024/25:108 Bilaga 5</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p816 ft15">Förslag till lag om ändring i lagen (1974:371) om rättegången i arbetstvister</P>
<P class="p817 ft2">Härigenom föreskrivs att 1 kap. 2 § lagen (1974:371) om rättegången i arbetstvister<SPAN class="ft17">1 </SPAN>ska ha följande lydelse.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t53">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr7 td16"><SPAN class="p13 ft3">Nuvarande lydelse</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr7 td17"><SPAN class="p13 ft16">Föreslagen lydelse</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p818 ft28">1 kap.</P>
<P class="p819 ft2">2 §<SPAN class="ft17">2</SPAN></P>
<P class="p820 ft2">Denna lag tillämpas inte på</P>
<P class="p821 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">mål som enligt lag får upptas endast av en viss tingsrätt eller som ska handläggas av en tingsrätt i en annan sammansättning än som anges i rättegångsbalken,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p822 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">mål som ska handläggas av tingsrätt med tillämpning av konkurslagen (1987:672) eller lagen (2022:964) om företagsrekonstruktion,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p822 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">mål om skadestånd i anledning av brott, om talan förs i samband med åtal för brottet,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p822 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">mål om ersättning för yrkesskada, när tvisten inte rör kollektivavtals rätta innebörd,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p822 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">mål som avses i 1 kap. 4 § 1 och 3 lagen (2016:188) om patent- och marknadsdomstolar, och</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t54">
<TR>
	<TD colspan=4 class="tr4 td16"><SPAN class="p33 ft2">6. mål som avses i artikel 81 i</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td25"><SPAN class="p15 ft2">6. mål som avses i artikel 81 i</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=4 class="tr5 td16"><SPAN class="p33 ft2">rådets förordning (EG) nr 6/2002</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td25"><SPAN class="p15 ft2">rådets förordning (EG) nr 6/2002</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td26"><SPAN class="p13 ft2">om</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr4 td60"><SPAN class="p13 ft3">gemenskapsformgivning</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td39"><SPAN class="p33 ft2">och</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td25"><SPAN class="p15 ft2">om <NOBR><SPAN class="ft3">EU-formgivning</SPAN></NOBR><SPAN class="ft3"> </SPAN>och artikel 124</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr4 td62"><SPAN class="p13 ft2">artikel 124</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr4 td63"><SPAN class="p33 ft2">i Europaparlamentets</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td25"><SPAN class="p16 ft2">i Europaparlamentets och rådets</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td26"><SPAN class="p13 ft2">och</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td55"><SPAN class="p50 ft2">rådets</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td125"><SPAN class="p65 ft2">förordning</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td39"><SPAN class="p33 ft2">(EU)</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td25"><SPAN class="p15 ft2">förordning (EU) 2017/1001 om</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD colspan=4 class="tr5 td16"><SPAN class="p13 ft2">2017/1001 om <NOBR>EU-varumärken.</NOBR></SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td25"><SPAN class="p823 ft2"><NOBR>EU-varumärken.</NOBR></SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p824 ft2">Lagen ska inte tillämpas på mål som rör arbetstagare som avses i 1 § lagen (1994:260) om offentlig anställning, när tvisten gäller</P>
<P class="p822 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft25">fråga som rör anställning av arbetstagare utan att enbart avse tvist om kollektivavtal,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p822 ft6"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft20">tjänstgöringsskyldighet för ordinarie domare enligt lagen (1994:261) om fullmaktsanställning.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p824 ft6">Lagen ska inte heller tillämpas på andra mål som rör arbetstagare hos arbetsgivare med offentlig ställning, när tvisten gäller en fråga som är reglerad i lag eller annan författning och det i samma författning föreskrivs att beslut i frågan får överklagas till regeringen, en förvaltningsdomstol eller en förvaltningsmyndighet.</P>
<P class="p825 ft2">Denna lag träder i kraft den 1 juni 2025.</P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t55">
<TR>
	<TD rowspan=2 class="tr10 td178"><SPAN class="p16 ft2">126</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td40"><SPAN class="p15 ft21">1</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td211"><SPAN class="p1 ft148">Lagen omtryckt 1977:530.</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr15 td40"><SPAN class="p15 ft21">2</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr15 td211"><SPAN class="p1 ft148">Senaste lydelse 2022:973.</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>

<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p12 ft1">Lagrådets yttrande</P>
<P class="p826 ft2">Utdrag protokoll vid sammanträde <NOBR>2025-02-06</NOBR></P>
<P class="p827 ft150"><SPAN class="ft149">Närvarande: </SPAN>F.d. justitieråden Eskil Nord och Sten Andersson samt justitierådet Marie Jönsson</P>
<P class="p828 ft28">Ändringar i EU:s formskyddsförordning</P>
<P class="p829 ft6">Enligt en lagrådsremiss den 30 januari 2025 har regeringen (Justitiedepartementet) beslutat inhämta Lagrådets yttrande över förslag till</P>
<P class="p55 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft32">lag om ändring i mönsterskyddslagen (1970:485),</SPAN></P>
<P class="p55 ft2"><SPAN class="ft2">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft32">lag om ändring i lagen (1974:371) om rättegången i arbetstvister.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p828 ft2">Förslagen har inför Lagrådet föredragits av ämnesrådet Patrik Sundberg.</P>
<P class="p830 ft2">Lagrådet lämnar förslagen utan erinran.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p76 ft4">Prop. 2024/25:108 Bilaga 6</P>
<P class="p811 ft2">127</P>
